 2552 happyNewToken action sts stk [] =
 2553         happyDoAction 52# notHappyAtAll action sts stk []
 2554 
 2555 happyNewToken action sts stk (tk:tks) =
 2556         let cont i = happyDoAction i tk action sts stk tks in
 2557         case tk of {
 2558         TReserved _ "import" -> cont 1#;
 2559         TReserved _ "and" -> cont 2#;
 2560         TReserved _ "as" -> cont 3#;
 2561         TReserved _ "hiding" -> cont 4#;
 2562         TReserved _ "let" -> cont 5#;
 2563         TReserved _ "rec" -> cont 6#;
 2564         TReserved _ "in" -> cont 7#;
 2565         TReserved _ "do" -> cont 8#;
 2566         TReserved _ "if" -> cont 9#;
 2567         TReserved _ "then" -> cont 10#;
 2568         TReserved _ "else" -> cont 11#;
 2569         TReserved _ "typedef" -> cont 12#;
 2570         TReserved _ "CryptolSetup" -> cont 13#;
 2571         TReserved _ "JavaSetup" -> cont 14#;
 2572         TReserved _ "LLVMSetup" -> cont 15#;
 2573         TReserved _ "MIRSetup" -> cont 16#;
 2574         TReserved _ "ProofScript" -> cont 17#;
 2575         TReserved _ "TopLevel" -> cont 18#;
 2576         TReserved _ "CrucibleSetup" -> cont 19#;
 2577         TReserved _ "CrucibleMethodSpec" -> cont 20#;
 2578         TReserved _ "LLVMSpec" -> cont 21#;
 2579         TReserved _ "JVMMethodSpec" -> cont 22#;
 2580         TReserved _ "JVMSpec" -> cont 23#;
 2581         TReserved _ "MIRSpec" -> cont 24#;
 2582         TReserved _ "Bool" -> cont 25#;
 2583         TReserved _ "Int" -> cont 26#;
 2584         TReserved _ "String" -> cont 27#;
 2585         TReserved _ "Term" -> cont 28#;
 2586         TReserved _ "Type" -> cont 29#;
 2587         TReserved _ "AIG" -> cont 30#;
 2588         TReserved _ "CFG" -> cont 31#;
 2589         TPunct    _ ";" -> cont 32#;
 2590         TPunct    _ "[" -> cont 33#;
 2591         TPunct    _ "]" -> cont 34#;
 2592         TPunct    _ "(" -> cont 35#;
 2593         TPunct    _ ")" -> cont 36#;
 2594         TPunct    _ "{" -> cont 37#;
 2595         TPunct    _ "}" -> cont 38#;
 2596         TPunct    _ ":" -> cont 39#;
 2597         TPunct    _ "," -> cont 40#;
 2598         TPunct    _ "." -> cont 41#;
 2599         TPunct    _ "\\" -> cont 42#;
 2600         TPunct    _ "=" -> cont 43#;
 2601         TPunct    _ "->" -> cont 44#;
 2602         TPunct    _ "<-" -> cont 45#;
 2603         TLit      _ _ -> cont 46#;
 2604         TCode     _ _ -> cont 47#;
 2605         TCType    _ _ -> cont 48#;
 2606         TNum      _ _ _ -> cont 49#;
 2607         TVar      _ _ -> cont 50#;
 2608         TEOF      _ _ -> cont 51#;
 2609         _ -> happyError' ((tk:tks), [])
 2610         }
 2611 
 2612 happyError_ explist 52# tk tks = happyError' (tks, explist)
 2613 happyError_ explist _ tk tks = happyError' ((tk:tks), explist)
 2614 
 2615 happyThen :: () => Either ParseError a -> (a -> Either ParseError b) -> Either ParseError b
 2616 happyThen = (Prelude.>>=)
 2617 happyReturn :: () => a -> Either ParseError a
 2618 happyReturn = (Prelude.return)
 2619 happyThen1 m k tks = (Prelude.>>=) m (\a -> k a tks)
 2620 happyReturn1 :: () => a -> b -> Either ParseError a
 2621 happyReturn1 = \a tks -> (Prelude.return) a
 2622 happyError' :: () => ([(Token Pos)], [Prelude.String]) -> Either ParseError a
 2623 happyError' = (\(tokens, _) -> parseError tokens)
 2624 parseModule tks = happySomeParser where
 2625  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 0# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap9 x') = happyOut9 x} in x'))
 2626 
 2627 parseStmt tks = happySomeParser where
 2628  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 1# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap10 x') = happyOut10 x} in x'))
 2629 
 2630 parseStmtSemi tks = happySomeParser where
 2631  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 2# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap11 x') = happyOut11 x} in x'))
 2632 
 2633 parseExpression tks = happySomeParser where
 2634  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 3# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap12 x') = happyOut12 x} in x'))
 2635 
 2636 parseSchema tks = happySomeParser where
 2637  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 4# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap13 x') = happyOut13 x} in x'))
 2638 
 2639 parseSchemaPattern tks = happySomeParser where
 2640  happySomeParser = happyThen (happyParse 5# tks) (\x -> happyReturn (let {(HappyWrap14 x') = happyOut14 x} in x'))
 2641 
 2642 happySeq = happyDontSeq
 2643 
 2644 
 2645 data ParseError
 2646   = UnexpectedEOF
 2647   | UnexpectedToken (Token Pos)
 2648   | InvalidPattern Expr
 2649   | EmptyBlock Pos
 2650   | InvalidBlock Pos
 2651 
 2652 instance Exception ParseError
 2653 
 2654 instance Show ParseError where
 2655   show e =
 2656     case e of
 2657       UnexpectedEOF     -> "Parse error: unexpected end of file"
 2658       UnexpectedToken t -> "Parse error at " ++ show (tokPos t) ++ ": Unexpected `" ++ unpack (tokStr t) ++ "'"
 2659         where Range _ sl sc el ec = tokPos t -- TODO show token span consistently
 2660       InvalidPattern x  -> "Parse error: invalid pattern " ++ pShow x
 2661       EmptyBlock pos -> show pos ++ ": do block must include at least one expression"
 2662       InvalidBlock pos -> show pos ++ ": do block must end with expression"
 2663 
 2664 parseError :: [Token Pos] -> Either ParseError b
 2665 parseError toks = case toks of
 2666   []    -> Left UnexpectedEOF
 2667   t : _ -> Left (UnexpectedToken t)
 2668 
 2669 -- | As seen by the parser, a "function name" is an arbitrary pattern.
 2670 --   This is because we use the same syntax for function and value bindings:
 2671 --   in "let (a, b) = e" the "(a, b)" can and should be an arbitrary pattern.
 2672 --   For functions it doesn't make sense for it to be anything but a plain
 2673 --   name, as in "let f () = e". You can write "let (a, b) () = e" and the
 2674 --   parser will accept it, but it won't typecheck.
 2675 --
 2676 --   This function extracts the actual name, if any, for annotating
 2677 --   the lambda expressions we turn further arguments into. It will
 2678 --   return Nothing if the name is something other than an actual
 2679 --   name, which is fine for value bindings since the result won't be
 2680 --   used and also fine for nonsense like "let (a, b) () = e" that'll
 2681 --   be rejected by the typechecker. The annotations in question are
 2682 --   used only at eval time.
 2683 --
 2684 --   Runs in the Maybe monad for convenience.
 2685 fixFunctionName :: Maybe Pattern -> Maybe Text
 2686 fixFunctionName mname = do
 2687   name <- mname
 2688   case name of
 2689       PWild {} -> Nothing
 2690       PVar _pos name _ty -> Just $ getVal name
 2691       PTuple {} -> Nothing
 2692 
 2693 buildFunction :: Maybe Pattern -> [Pattern] -> Expr -> Expr
 2694 buildFunction mname args e =
 2695   let mname' = fixFunctionName mname
 2696       once :: Pattern -> Expr -> Expr
 2697       once pat e = Lambda (maxSpan' pat e) mname' pat e
 2698   in
 2699   foldr once e args
 2700 
 2701 buildApplication :: [Expr] -> Expr
 2702 buildApplication es =
 2703   foldl1 (\e body -> Application (maxSpan' e body) e body) es
 2704 
 2705 -- | Pop off the last statement in a do-block, which is required to
 2706 --   be a plain expression, and unpack it to an expression.
 2707 buildBlock :: Pos -> [Stmt] -> Either ParseError Expr
 2708 buildBlock pos stmts = case reverse stmts of
 2709   StmtBind _spos (PWild _patpos _noty) e : revstmts' ->
 2710     Right $ Block pos (reverse revstmts', e)
 2711   [] ->
 2712     Left $ EmptyBlock pos
 2713   _ ->
 2714     Left $ InvalidBlock pos
 2715 
 2716 toPattern :: Expr -> Either ParseError Pattern
 2717 toPattern expr =
 2718   case expr of
 2719     Tuple pos es       -> PTuple pos `fmap` mapM toPattern es
 2720     TSig pos (Var x) t -> return (PVar pos x (Just t))
 2721     Var x              -> return (PVar (getPos x) x Nothing)
 2722     _              -> Left (InvalidPattern expr)
 2723 
 2724 toLName :: Token Pos -> LName
 2725 toLName p = Located (tokStr p) (tokStr p) (tokPos p)

 2741 -- Do not remove this comment. Required to fix CPP parsing when using GCC and a clang-compiled alex.
 2742 #if __GLASGOW_HASKELL__ > 706
 2743 #define LT(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.<# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2744 #define GTE(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.>=# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2745 #define EQ(n,m) ((Happy_GHC_Exts.tagToEnum# (n Happy_GHC_Exts.==# m)) :: Prelude.Bool)
 2746 #else
 2747 #define LT(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.<# m)
 2748 #define GTE(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.>=# m)
 2749 #define EQ(n,m) (n Happy_GHC_Exts.==# m)
 2750 #endif

 2811 infixr 9 `HappyStk`
 2812 data HappyStk a = HappyStk a (HappyStk a)
 2813 
 2814 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2815 -- starting the parse
 2816 
 2817 happyParse start_state = happyNewToken start_state notHappyAtAll notHappyAtAll
 2818 
 2819 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2820 -- Accepting the parse
 2821 
 2822 -- If the current token is ERROR_TOK, it means we've just accepted a partial
 2823 -- parse (a %partial parser).  We must ignore the saved token on the top of
 2824 -- the stack in this case.
 2825 happyAccept 0# tk st sts (_ `HappyStk` ans `HappyStk` _) =
 2826         happyReturn1 ans
 2827 happyAccept j tk st sts (HappyStk ans _) = 
 2828         (happyTcHack j (happyTcHack st)) (happyReturn1 ans)
 2829 
 2830 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2831 -- Arrays only: do the next action
 2832 
 2833 
 2834 
 2835 happyDoAction i tk st
 2836         = {- nothing -}
 2837           case action of
 2838                 0#           -> {- nothing -}
 2839                                      happyFail (happyExpListPerState ((Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (st)) :: Prelude.Int)) i tk st
 2840                 -1#          -> {- nothing -}
 2841                                      happyAccept i tk st
 2842                 n | LT(n,(0# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) -> {- nothing -}
 2843                                                    (happyReduceArr Happy_Data_Array.! rule) i tk st
 2844                                                    where rule = (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# ((Happy_GHC_Exts.negateInt# ((n Happy_GHC_Exts.+# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))))))
 2845                 n                 -> {- nothing -}
 2846                                      happyShift new_state i tk st
 2847                                      where new_state = (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))
 2848    where off    = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyActOffsets st)
 2849          off_i  = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# i)
 2850          check  = if GTE(off_i,(0# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#))
 2851                   then EQ(indexShortOffAddr happyCheck off_i, i)
 2852                   else Prelude.False
 2853          action
 2854           | check     = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 2855           | Prelude.otherwise = indexShortOffAddr happyDefActions st
 2856 
 2857 
 2858 
 2859 
 2860 indexShortOffAddr (HappyA# arr) off =
 2861         Happy_GHC_Exts.narrow16Int# i
 2862   where
 2863         i = Happy_GHC_Exts.word2Int# (Happy_GHC_Exts.or# (Happy_GHC_Exts.uncheckedShiftL# high 8#) low)
 2864         high = Happy_GHC_Exts.int2Word# (Happy_GHC_Exts.ord# (Happy_GHC_Exts.indexCharOffAddr# arr (off' Happy_GHC_Exts.+# 1#)))
 2865         low  = Happy_GHC_Exts.int2Word# (Happy_GHC_Exts.ord# (Happy_GHC_Exts.indexCharOffAddr# arr off'))
 2866         off' = off Happy_GHC_Exts.*# 2#
 2867 
 2868 
 2869 
 2870 
 2871 {-# INLINE happyLt #-}
 2872 happyLt x y = LT(x,y)                                                             
 2873 
 2874 
 2875 readArrayBit arr bit =
 2876     Bits.testBit (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (indexShortOffAddr arr ((unbox_int bit) `Happy_GHC_Exts.iShiftRA#` 4#))) (bit `Prelude.mod` 16)
 2877   where unbox_int (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# x) = x
 2878 
 2879 
 2880 
 2881 
 2882 
 2883 
 2884 data HappyAddr = HappyA# Happy_GHC_Exts.Addr#

 2888 -- HappyState data type (not arrays)

 2902 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2903 -- Shifting a token
 2904 
 2905 happyShift new_state 0# tk st sts stk@(x `HappyStk` _) =
 2906      let i = (case Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# x of { (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i)) -> i }) in
 2907 --     trace "shifting the error token" $
 2908      happyDoAction i tk new_state (HappyCons (st) (sts)) (stk)
 2909 
 2910 happyShift new_state i tk st sts stk =
 2911      happyNewToken new_state (HappyCons (st) (sts)) ((happyInTok (tk))`HappyStk`stk)
 2912 
 2913 -- happyReduce is specialised for the common cases.
 2914 
 2915 happySpecReduce_0 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2916      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2917 happySpecReduce_0 nt fn j tk st@((action)) sts stk
 2918      = happyGoto nt j tk st (HappyCons (st) (sts)) (fn `HappyStk` stk)
 2919 
 2920 happySpecReduce_1 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2921      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2922 happySpecReduce_1 nt fn j tk _ sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))) (v1`HappyStk`stk')
 2923      = let r = fn v1 in
 2924        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 2925 
 2926 happySpecReduce_2 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2927      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2928 happySpecReduce_2 nt fn j tk _ (HappyCons (_) (sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))))) (v1`HappyStk`v2`HappyStk`stk')
 2929      = let r = fn v1 v2 in
 2930        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 2931 
 2932 happySpecReduce_3 i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2933      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2934 happySpecReduce_3 nt fn j tk _ (HappyCons (_) ((HappyCons (_) (sts@((HappyCons (st@(action)) (_))))))) (v1`HappyStk`v2`HappyStk`v3`HappyStk`stk')
 2935      = let r = fn v1 v2 v3 in
 2936        happySeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st sts (r `HappyStk` stk'))
 2937 
 2938 happyReduce k i fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2939      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2940 happyReduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk
 2941      = case happyDrop (k Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) sts of
 2942          sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 2943                 let r = fn stk in  -- it doesn't hurt to always seq here...
 2944                 happyDoSeq r (happyGoto nt j tk st1 sts1 r)
 2945 
 2946 happyMonadReduce k nt fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2947      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2948 happyMonadReduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk =
 2949       case happyDrop k (HappyCons (st) (sts)) of
 2950         sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 2951           let drop_stk = happyDropStk k stk in
 2952           happyThen1 (fn stk tk) (\r -> happyGoto nt j tk st1 sts1 (r `HappyStk` drop_stk))
 2953 
 2954 happyMonad2Reduce k nt fn 0# tk st sts stk
 2955      = happyFail [] 0# tk st sts stk
 2956 happyMonad2Reduce k nt fn j tk st sts stk =
 2957       case happyDrop k (HappyCons (st) (sts)) of
 2958         sts1@((HappyCons (st1@(action)) (_))) ->
 2959          let drop_stk = happyDropStk k stk
 2960 
 2961              off = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyGotoOffsets st1)
 2962              off_i = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# nt)
 2963              new_state = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 2964 
 2965 
 2966 
 2967 
 2968           in
 2969           happyThen1 (fn stk tk) (\r -> happyNewToken new_state sts1 (r `HappyStk` drop_stk))
 2970 
 2971 happyDrop 0# l = l
 2972 happyDrop n (HappyCons (_) (t)) = happyDrop (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1# :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) t
 2973 
 2974 happyDropStk 0# l = l
 2975 happyDropStk n (x `HappyStk` xs) = happyDropStk (n Happy_GHC_Exts.-# (1#::Happy_GHC_Exts.Int#)) xs
 2976 
 2977 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2978 -- Moving to a new state after a reduction
 2979 
 2980 
 2981 happyGoto nt j tk st = 
 2982    {- nothing -}
 2983    happyDoAction j tk new_state
 2984    where off = happyAdjustOffset (indexShortOffAddr happyGotoOffsets st)
 2985          off_i = (off Happy_GHC_Exts.+# nt)
 2986          new_state = indexShortOffAddr happyTable off_i
 2987 
 2988 
 2989 
 2990 
 2991 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 2992 -- Error recovery (ERROR_TOK is the error token)
 2993 
 2994 -- parse error if we are in recovery and we fail again
 2995 happyFail explist 0# tk old_st _ stk@(x `HappyStk` _) =
 2996      let i = (case Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# x of { (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i)) -> i }) in
 2997 --      trace "failing" $ 
 2998         happyError_ explist i tk
 2999 
 3000 {-  We don't need state discarding for our restricted implementation of
 3001     "error".  In fact, it can cause some bogus parses, so I've disabled it
 3002     for now --SDM
 3003 
 3004 -- discard a state
 3005 happyFail  ERROR_TOK tk old_st CONS(HAPPYSTATE(action),sts) 
 3006                                                 (saved_tok `HappyStk` _ `HappyStk` stk) =
 3007 --      trace ("discarding state, depth " ++ show (length stk))  $
 3008         DO_ACTION(action,ERROR_TOK,tk,sts,(saved_tok`HappyStk`stk))
 3009 -}
 3010 
 3011 -- Enter error recovery: generate an error token,
 3012 --                       save the old token and carry on.
 3013 happyFail explist i tk (action) sts stk =
 3014 --      trace "entering error recovery" $
 3015         happyDoAction 0# tk action sts ((Happy_GHC_Exts.unsafeCoerce# (Happy_GHC_Exts.I# (i))) `HappyStk` stk)
 3016 
 3017 -- Internal happy errors:
 3018 
 3019 notHappyAtAll :: a
 3020 notHappyAtAll = Prelude.error "Internal Happy error\n"
 3021 
 3022 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3023 -- Hack to get the typechecker to accept our action functions
 3024 
 3025 
 3026 happyTcHack :: Happy_GHC_Exts.Int# -> a -> a
 3027 happyTcHack x y = y
 3028 {-# INLINE happyTcHack #-}

 3031 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3032 -- Seq-ing.  If the --strict flag is given, then Happy emits 
 3033 --      happySeq = happyDoSeq
 3034 -- otherwise it emits
 3035 --      happySeq = happyDontSeq
 3036 
 3037 happyDoSeq, happyDontSeq :: a -> b -> b
 3038 happyDoSeq   a b = a `Prelude.seq` b
 3039 happyDontSeq a b = b
 3040 
 3041 -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
 3042 -- Don't inline any functions from the template.  GHC has a nasty habit
 3043 -- of deciding to inline happyGoto everywhere, which increases the size of
 3044 -- the generated parser quite a bit.
 3045 
 3046 
 3047 {-# NOINLINE happyDoAction #-}
 3048 {-# NOINLINE happyTable #-}
 3049 {-# NOINLINE happyCheck #-}
 3050 {-# NOINLINE happyActOffsets #-}
 3051 {-# NOINLINE happyGotoOffsets #-}
 3052 {-# NOINLINE happyDefActions #-}
 3053 
 3054 {-# NOINLINE happyShift #-}
 3055 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_0 #-}
 3056 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_1 #-}
 3057 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_2 #-}
 3058 {-# NOINLINE happySpecReduce_3 #-}
 3059 {-# NOINLINE happyReduce #-}
 3060 {-# NOINLINE happyMonadReduce #-}
 3061 {-# NOINLINE happyGoto #-}
